- **Node 12**: Access to 🌾10, 🐑5, 🐑11. Good diversity and high production probability.

- **Node 33**: Access to 🌾10, 🌾5. Limited diversity but high production probability.

Considering resource diversity, production probability, and future expansion potential, **Node 11** stands out as a strong candidate. It provides access to wheat (🌾10), sheep (🐑12, 🐑5), and is well-positioned for future expansion. Additionally, it is close to the 2:1 wheat port at nodes 32 and 33, which can be beneficial for trading.

1. **Current Plan**: Build the initial settlement at Node 11, then focus on expanding towards high-probability tiles and ports.

   - [1] Build a road at edge (10, 11)

3. **Resource Collection**:
   - The settlement at Node 11 produces: 🧱4[⭐], 🐑12, 🌾10[⭐]
   - High-probability tiles nearby: 🌾10 (-1, -1, 2), 🧱4 (0, -1, 1), 🌲8 (1, -1, 0)

4. **Strategic Considerations**:
   - **Action [0]**: Building a road at edge (11, 12) would connect to Node 12, which is adjacent to 🌾10 and 🧱4. This is beneficial as it allows for potential expansion towards high-probability tiles.
   - **Action [1]**: Building a road at edge (10, 11) would connect to Node 10, which is adjacent to 🧱4 and 🐑12. This is also beneficial but slightly less optimal than Action [0] because it doesn't directly connect to the high-probability 🌾10 tile.
   - **Action [2]**: Building a road at edge (11, 32) would connect to Node 32, which is adjacent to 🐑12 and 🌾10. This is a good option as it connects to high-probability tiles and also opens up the possibility of using the 2:1 🌾 WHEAT Port at nodes {32, 33}.

5. **Next 2-3 Turns**:
   - Building towards Node 32 allows for better resource trading and potential settlement expansion.
   - Connecting to Node 12 also provides good resource opportunities but without the immediate port access.

6. **Final Decision**:
   - Building a road at edge (11, 32) is the best option as it connects to high-probability tiles and provides access to a 2:1 port, which can be crucial for resource management in the early game.

   - Moving the robber to (1, 1, -2) blocks the 🏜️- tile, which does not produce resources.

   - Moving the robber to (2, -1, -1) blocks the 🌲5 tile, which affects RED.

### Conclusion:
The best action is to move the robber to (2, -1, -1) and steal from RED. This blocks the 🌲5 tile, which is crucial for RED's city at node 23, and allows BLUE to steal a resource from RED.

   - **[2] Trade 4 🐑SHEEP for 1 🌾WHEAT**:
     - We already have 1 🌾WHEAT, and getting more 🌾WHEAT is not immediately beneficial.
   - **[3] Trade 4 🐑SHEEP for 1 🌲WOOD**:
     - 🌲WOOD is crucial for building roads and settlements. This trade will help us continue our plan to build roads towards the 🌾 WHEAT Port.
   - **[4] Trade 4 🐑SHEEP for 1 🧱BRICK**:
     - We already have 1 🧱BRICK, and getting more 🧱BRICK is not immediately beneficial.

### Decision:
